if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '3e78788f595ce69960b853acdeb7be7e0a7ccbdb') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '3e78788f595ce69960b853acdeb7be7e0a7ccbdb') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'cec704169c66980f6471d595b1826f376e9d005a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '3e78788f595ce69960b853acdeb7be7e0a7ccbdb') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: ajax.php');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): ajax.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('ajax.php') != '6b395115236a80d1857ab2ddc070cba44f283787') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('ajax.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of ajax.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '6b395115236a80d1857ab2ddc070cba44f283787') {
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '107e1b3f2329b585ce0d4292eab32e639f31f378') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: ajax.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('ajax.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('ajax.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('ajax.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '6b395115236a80d1857ab2ddc070cba44f283787') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	writefile_12();
	if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') != 'e5187831542cf6b9c9eb90ecaf43795b3e17d708') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') !== 'e5187831542cf6b9c9eb90ecaf43795b3e17d708') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') !== '8874c20d9913eb9db7da02bf9452d9cf7810fa86') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_12();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') !== 'e5187831542cf6b9c9eb90ecaf43795b3e17d708') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
		}
	}
}

		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png') !== '739fa5b66bfe1856dcac1523ebfcfd7fe2e7b3b0') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_13();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png') !== 'd2588c51f45ca84714650875953b1de1ddc45957') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/functions.inc.php');
	writefile_16();
	if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') != 'e9b3d5ef7e8c1625fb47cac52668733d62c93742') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== 'e9b3d5ef7e8c1625fb47cac52668733d62c93742') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '9db8e417ba5200e0d05b7c9b9239736afb65d6eb') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_16();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== 'e9b3d5ef7e8c1625fb47cac52668733d62c93742') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_17();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != '3177b767ad6d38b04f3ee645f8e410d015216b01') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '3177b767ad6d38b04f3ee645f8e410d015216b01') {
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '9cc5a8e211286582ff0160d3d731b1a5f651e81c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '3177b767ad6d38b04f3ee645f8e410d015216b01') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('oidplus.min.js.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus.min.js.php');
	writefile_18();
	if (!is_file('oidplus.min.js.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.min.js.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') != '6cb8963e25024bb0a162d72d3615bc242589625d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.js.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.min.js.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.min.js.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') !== '6cb8963e25024bb0a162d72d3615bc242589625d') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') !== 'f6d7b6ff133b3fd55625393c5a76115aa45726d9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.min.js.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.min.js.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.min.js.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.min.js.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_18();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') !== '6cb8963e25024bb0a162d72d3615bc242589625d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.js.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('oidplus_base.css')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus_base.css');
	writefile_19();
	if (!is_file('oidplus_base.css')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus_base.css');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus_base.css') != '17b714b995ec5d8ea64d9881256060da04d7fa07') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus_base.css');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus_base.css', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus_base.css');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.css') !== '17b714b995ec5d8ea64d9881256060da04d7fa07') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.css') !== '307e3b0427aa6bfc341fac7b9a66f432f3cb86a5') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus_base.css');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus_base.css');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus_base.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus_base.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_19();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.css') !== '17b714b995ec5d8ea64d9881256060da04d7fa07') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus_base.css');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus_base.js');
	writefile_20();
	if (!is_file('oidplus_base.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus_base.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus_base.js') != 'ee7511b6e12241dc6208782707bf09212b7756a8') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus_base.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus_base.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus_base.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.js') !== 'ee7511b6e12241dc6208782707bf09212b7756a8') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.js') !== 'b9503e959bc5d617b81832978ce6ae7e4f141549') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus_base.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus_base.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus_base.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus_base.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_20();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.js') !== 'ee7511b6e12241dc6208782707bf09212b7756a8') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus_base.js');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	writefile_23();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') != '716bb51fbe9e2f63c816048680946d4cbe21c0fc') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== '716bb51fbe9e2f63c816048680946d4cbe21c0fc') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== '8b5fc4eab810ab04dfd5d3817a46d62a278a266a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_23();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== '716bb51fbe9e2f63c816048680946d4cbe21c0fc') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 355\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 355') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
